Viewable Currency


Brand campaign-focused ad industry professionals have been complaining about clickthroughs as a lousy metric for premium marketing. Engagement is the buzzword, but how to measure it in a way everyone agrees is has been the problematic response. Peter Naylor, EVP, Digital Media Sales for NBCUniversal (and IAB Chairman), casts his vote for viewable impressions as the new standard for figuring out a placement's value. "When advertisers know their ads are visible, when they see a rise in performance, when we have conversations based on the reality that there is a finite amount of valuable advertising space online, and when we are able to make apples-to-apples comparisons with other media that rely on viewability measures, advertiser confidence in buying display ads increases," he writes in Ad Age. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGfQpTN6qJk0VFcGREuJoOqKnwZT1aVc3lyfcltQmVXa72qj23iZok340E-KkqqWf1vkM1KwYrvcBGtYqB-wi4FRZPno0OHaQmTusdgrY0LNhJnOVtrsKx_kvNMn22MmL38upAifJmHqrTOJdj0pD-5v_T7rgGn-sF_wacRbHbtKofwXrciNo983zo6IAJT-W6fJPQ6EmSGp_A==> . 


Eye On Mobile Ads


A feature article in The Wall Street Journal looks at the different ways mobile advertising is being implemented today by marketers. The WSJ concludes, "Marketers and ad-dependent companies said banner ads are an inevitable first step in a new ad medium, just as the first wave of the Internet was dominated by now notorious pop-up and 'dancing cowboy' ads." Dancing cowboy? It was "Shoot the Monkey!" Read more (subscription). <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGdLnHmDAGqFrKaUqLR5QZe4bl2CPwvw-KIjqmq4YWtZvNJIpPFDTWnaSE2LhehFraTS6lsbFqzwabYZEIcztBXROSFFvW_OMZc5I23Y3ZP4MIYSeAU60WdzCRJWAe06ZSZ8Lr48rLkgU9YBpo8vaxp5AjqYPSjgevos7-FY6YbhfaPwTx5kSBKm> 


Klout's Audience Platform


Microsoft will bring Bing search data to Klout's "audience platform" of influencers, as part of as part of a strategic investment in the company. Klout CEO Joe Fernandez writes in a blog post, "Search data has long been one of the missing signals in our effort to fully recognize a person's influence. Just as Wikipedia articles can reflect a person's real world influence, search results for a person signal accomplishments achieved beyond social networks and serve to influence others... This is a small step for Bing and Klout towards a very big idea: search through people." Read it.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGd33Kud86WqIeIv84QVKMX7vD11clPAB_PzTwI1pYCS2vrvr5M78HT22aqxmqcSWi8VrDpyRtTMBpIC7QmWWVAwzm2xzr-PMV2zmUsgvPFdzdnj4sjBw9POhYtOSmnIxMP6dOjC9r3lA4hVlo-6RzAY> 


The Wrong Incentive?


Competition must be getting pretty tense among ad networks these days. How else to explain SocialVibe's attempt to entice new clients with a raffle? As Digiday's Jack Marshall reports <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGdn71SQ-gw7KIK0utVnR-ddoph-c3jyh34JZGSrW1mjLP0lh39j5LW4V8BYbA6-jUx77MIb6zqRa9uNGlASyqzhJW_TfMbrBIGGpZLVq4iVHxUl4sDX0aRqieRV3sVw_39ya4xu6H7uXFuvgvCIEtMbG_1ChIrQ7tyzc-UQ1c_8-Q==> , the social ad network offered media buyers who share their contact info with them the chance to win a free first class trip to Las Vegas, where they would stay at a penthouse suite, all expenses paid. SocialVibe CMO John Capano defended the offer, saying, "It's just a lead-gen campaign... We don't do any of the Hamptons houses or anything like that, and we're very much against it. We draw the line at pens and beer koozies, and taking clients to dinner." 


The Publisher Fix


Yieldbot CEO Jonathan Mendez makes a pitch on the company's blog and doesn't mince words about the publisher predicament today. He writes, "What we're seeing from Yahoo is representative of the change that Publishers must make in order to survive. Bringing in one of the sharpest minds on Search as CEO to help save the struggling web banner company should be a beacon to all publishers. Your business is a utility. You deliver valuable content. That includes advertising. The value of that advertising is based on the quality of your audience to the advertiser as measured by a performance metric..." Patience Over Innovation


The problems affecting digital media and advertising is not that there's too little innovation. It's that there's too little patience with the pace of it. So says Rob Norman, Global Chief Digital Officer for WPP's GroupM, who tells The Makegood's Matt Straz: "Our clients operate at scale and innovation is only relevant if it has the potential to make a difference to business results...This is no insurance against failure but it is insurance against passing on long term opportunities because of short term disappointment." Read the rest <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGfY5v2kO38v73H1KfnQpjhe502494zzBcSiRSTvZs2I-SjXP2bUg5J3PA-Yon97v7VMIeLDRCfuLud7ugIPQYyDYOgBhBA6Y82V-JIZbLU0ICVV7Im_8pACK3OJGXODdP3kgV789LV6ZlqfL_WPyiTMyyWqLHGTltPr4iWL6lexIg8ZGcnMEWTemzBi2563pQrSYxiH4oDULA==> . 


Retargeting Upgrade


The world has left "Retargeting 1.0" behind, writes Eric Porres in iMediaConnection. What's 2.0? For starters, oh so dynamic. "Technologies analyze prospect's behavior: how many times they've seen an ad, whether they've responded, and how they've responded." Prospects are grouped and regrouped into categories based on their real-time actions. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGcqJZ8CDfFvp8bIZXGHNQYtZTm3ejIovtrFjkyptlUDy27jnJ5nJ0z5PGOBaTIIq562xf37DhHu6jITU3enoiLb8IZurnHccIPPA5JG_XUUzHNG2oBRUPi5d9CIaHgVqz8IoijycjtvJg==>  


Publishers: Agencies Have Attitude


UK-based Association of Online Publishers (AOP) said earlier this week that according to results of its latest survey agencies aren't helping publishers' mobile cause. From the AOP's site, "Nearly twice as many respondents to the Census said agency attitude rather than audience size would hold back mobile revenue growth next year, cited by 55% and 31% respectively. Dependency on low-yield ad networks would also hamper growth, according to 52%." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t3CJdWqPYGeF4bQj0oESJAxUw9KB8J5a2N_wvZOkPFOQB4rKYIHF-56XL5kVnsZoQGWxZZzGa_Wb-Ot1eLlE-zxAJOey3F_eSIh5m2PgdxEcLRjc1SU9HPI-sutgFJbOCi4l7k6ZKY9raU5mc75-W7xKRrvLsQAWzbTvUks18lfI3Ed8hz9Z_nSwBvtKpgRXJNmZZN99GrUhiZUyXa5_7ZKGY91zkRvUFCpOyJdhw-GgAoU8QhaTBA==> .

Looking For 'Acqui-hires'


Yahoo's "Marissa Mayer era" is starting to take shape with a series of small moves that are designed to change the culture at the portal. For example, Blackberries are out, iPhones are in. The "biggest" change is yet to come, as Mayer seeks a few good "acqui-hires." But one alleged prospect wasn't impresssed, telling the NYT's Nicole Perlroth,Yahoo failed to do due diligence. "At Facebook and Google, they know your underwear size before you walk in the door," this person said. "At Yahoo, it was clear they hadn't even Googled me." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE6p9FAjpV4HBBCHTOh4eRKPgjSAAy16U9czdm9LV-dJSS-VQVwTuCoCJ1cglKnd6BBhmzOSIfmRZ0MsK-sbKBi8R4EoTCs1eXFdoZ8iw7tAJZijnt_OEhIcvOrbCnNbYUmbZu0Ox7UNg8Fl1pQe2l0zdKQTupOL62NgKRa0G9EbPuzGGfDQOHlO_a0QnTz7tIhbsdL_YeixeNqqRgnsRwTLTsj3kCUDOfR10vgQXGEROz-RwsbIQyMg9RscGNj7yac=> . 


First-Party Display


Neustar announced that it's putting first-party, CRM data to work in online display advertising with a new product it's calling ConsumerReach, "an attribute matching solution." The press release explains that the product gives "consumer brands the ability to reach prospects and retain, up-sell and reinforce awareness among their best current customers with precise messaging across multiple online display advertising platforms without compromising consumer privacy. It also offers post campaign analysis..." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE7N8VNpf__vW0Pzd0HKa3g49mkD3p0hqtEhhzsccTBSKv7zw4d71VC4yueDYyNLdpEiaFYiP_bT1ErxZh5WjZxUUsB2TJUM8nDSNShUPZfYctC80VPDZtUr-qECENjgdDZqcY4yC0ymFBNCSt3acQHI>  


PointRoll Video Gets 'InTagrated'


Gannett rich media ad provider PointRoll is introducing a new product called InTagration, which is designed to ensure that in-stream video campaigns work seamlessly across all devices and formats. "So essentially, if you are running a multi-channel in-stream video campaign with a media buy on multiple publishers with different requirements, your life just got easier," writes Kailei Richardson, PointRoll's director of marketing, in a blog post. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE7cGHMvUaAmoObZGVlOBk9gIdxZeKKdWpgIaanyKrQyIvA0sTYZCm4Kd6J15n2tvVuvmrX366ThW0QT169CpjyTjUL1NlYpXpmNtHBnZBiYQS7E2cO3cCTdWVTt_1eSKpFZUpLfXvkd3mKsjIswdLyu1xChadIs0a7oMtidl0Sz_DgUQTfZQVmMi5a3m5V-AGg6a_tgIwG9uw==> . The message: make video ad delivery easier at-scale. 


Facebook Ad Net


Business Insider brings some fresh speculation on a Facebook RTB display ad network. Now that it has a mobile ad network in testing (AdExchanger story <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE6IrLDtifsnXII4Zo8QVz3wFAP4QR6-8IFMDIAq4S7o8sYqil8kaSZaOpn5LvovNFxPYP4dgWNOpRoCW4RMFjGR3PI53Bx7yjxZuWlNH1qfq-uWUNaYQByhkKxOj9RlWJPW2CxHM29ESLOSzHR1inXpRZn7JI6xD0qw_eSbui-09g==> ), Jim Edwards proposes the desktop version is a logical next step. He enforces the point of view with a comment from Rubicon's Frank Addante, fresh from seeing Facebook ad architect Gokul Rajaram speak at AdExchanger's Human Centered Automation conference. Addante tells him, "If Facebook is able to leverage its data but do so on high-quality content, it's really very powerful." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE6bW69eU1ZUux2u3gRMJ1mtpJSg8pFzW30wG151DtFCll7zhRkcVq-Q9pBisAAw0svC-Kyeq8Iu0qJzi5WMRe-POS0Jhu207BOc8lp0tjqGdlZT5xJ0NVUNOfD3L4H5LMrle4jpFnaQwVE2GS8ONbKi3S3ALEPISb0N33JotaPswpD65DAj4MeBswUYZoPF71mTOYtYn5i86MVAJ4UqNJHc>  


INTJ


Doug Weaver reflects on the power of the introvert on the digital sales team. Loud mouths may need to rethink their selling strategy as he writes, "In the workshops I conduct with sales teams I have started to look for the introverts and carefully draw out their ideas and solutions. Having spent a little more time in their own heads, their thinking is almost always more complete." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE6hAXBlmNrYgRmbF36CxT0p2icfh_CJAfWULItJZ_tc0Dk3wYCj85MZRNDgesiW0jfvn1wYgFZhhbINgOTsjOgPpw6yOnOlvOrG5SUOyk-UeMdGdy3v0HmH>

Vibrant Revamp


Vibrant Media's name is synonymous with in-line contextual ads, but users curse those ads almost as often as they click them. Writes AdAge's Michael Learmonth, "Vibrant is hoping to change that with a host of new formats using video, images and social content, but to also ask a bit more politely before they take over the screen." Also, the price model is shifting from CPC to cost-per-engagement. Read more.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001cwgN_sryOE56Dh1UreXQpTLho_vNkbgxcopkdEq0fz9r7HW_N4dnYr8D96rnWhB5Wvg42oq3vKWQFOSm-QgcnhfDNLJZ44F4IfTFctHf_lJG86xZDb5yCuuonNR_ZXSmwebhGTHAj2nnHr48yxt3lTYMk6UeVYDfsQT0CHu3HWGpRdoTgVj26eZSBjk27QjgxW_aJ862lPs=>

Criteo's Windfall


Retargeting specialist Criteo has been working on its expansion plans lately and has its eye on building up its presence. The company has raised a whopping $38 million (30 million euros) fourth round funding from its recent partner <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8xml6g_-DbFKKk_-OS0SRSw2ad8qbRCP7CUFZcrnjWIDqqZ2JGjCEKOQzU_VeOMgez3hNbGL7Byt98fTdKKdlIUjRINcvLVgzKyJn0MJgOU2GiF65076zzaafwjK4pAZZe1bH29eC1A9yoWFkltV3fQfiAhUUr36mogtW283Op5pGkNv0S0l6m8Oqtb_JNy81xtPqbXI_NTI03-x3LTG3jfW0tl3GkoDT76VO68ZP4oE3QEQS9--rbd>  Yahoo Japan. The large size of the round is likely to spur speculation about Criteo's plans: was this done to pay off investors? Is it a bridge loan? A Criteo rep told us it's neither and that it's strictly to build up its tech offerings and scaling the global expansion. "We've been profitable for three years, so a loan is not needed," the rep said. Read more on AllThingsD. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8x1A6qIw-KYUe6z0Vsc6n_6DQWue3b9lZZms1sHRlmjUDwIEe505W1TSSjCJ1mZ6Tw_xQM8Yc_ZaiEhhlAjlH_PONvb_j8mGcR4m0knz-MSp8Mcsk1ZoaaJEFYH2jG9ptmOSwo3v5H15mIX1PpO-WYZCAA2NMxMMO2hhn_q-UQgemds6RU0MWygXsxz5GitdkaIcQMG5jEP6g==> 


FBX Ads: Your Way, Right Away


A new stat from Facebook Exchange partner Triggit suggests FBX may be great for short consideration purchases. Steve Palombo writes in a Triggit blog post, "A majority (60%) of the visitors who we found on FBX showed up for auction on Facebook's exchange within 60 minutes of visiting a partner's site." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8xOghNchf5EkefwwvJqMoAOgVVgL4zm2Fzn_HLE3OnuzoXpr7EYY_KfI6uuMr_T8jgHhy8_jekNxz2jVGgnSpS6ekOsLSISFZE5OrMaasbQp2zwWrJ5LyPIJZG_5VF-gA0ihjbXXr4BLVmIdUekjtq6psgmS6Zau9A=>  Triggit has lately pivoted to be the "Facebook DSP," and in an interview with Business Insider's Nicholas Carlson, CEO Zach Coelius gets bullish. "When Coelius says that 18 months from now, most of Facebook's ad inventory will be sold through retargeting, and that rates will have gone up by a couple multiples, we find him to be credible enough." More. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8xyt5Eh2YejsctcQboDej6PbRmZKd2U72K9sVrhuz2wBMgtHKu-51lW4wURRWPqLz6kFkWw90CGdd9zhvmT5JTR70iaqwKrn1ZwwecII2cRy70wYrgLg66D7dKymOquAdMwbqClCy0j4g==>  


The Atlantic's Banner Ban


Jay Lauf, The Atlantic's publisher, isn't exactly declaring war on banner ads, but he is trying his best to de-emphasize the format in favor of the news and culture magazine site's "native ads." He tells Digiday's Josh Sternberg, "I would love to eliminate banners because I think most of them don't work. There's a need for scalable solution for certain advertisers. What I'm advocating is more relevant, engaging content." Read the rest <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8y7JwUapRH7ycNrjdi6zRD5WoMVCLp6BDXz2HJMeUv4x_i03-bIK1GJ0NWIfHb7PohMBJmNjemC9PP1AYLArUyqoqZG2s2B6ifK765quB6jlxrJ_pIHqcorOmsONi9tuyfUbGXi_34p9c4gk3sX3Fl-vt7i-QOFM8A=> . 


When To Spend $20 Million


In an interview with Boston Business Journal, HubSpot CEO Brian Halligan (AdExchanger Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8xwkbX0bE3hZbd2BFJSrhofmfFpNd1QHD4H_CGKhevCIinpH3Cqtot7MJQOWFIb1AXnGwnqQvkMmHrMD52d5bwfrzbDKpv28eogZr2e_SoCUi-TbEtgX5rbjdu2MxIGylNyAY-d-l8Omw==> &A in June) divulges the $20 million acquisition price for landing page optimizer Performable last year <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8wb7aFebdX2F1v0466iu8w774bMuoEbiz1xNO5WUJOdQo-iTPT1-po85_6QsDjGEaxzgp-AmBybH3M5cQs7TcZxzpC-yAqJ9BpSGc4OfCO3DAACkkkvAxU16vQhQpmo___oEYRnsp4YJ-hPRduXn5sCY3u1qbKSRKebjTk1f5Fouw==> . Halligan goes on to say that even though it was an expensive deal, it was necessary: "If I had to criticize HubSpot, in the early days of HubSpot, we were very good at sales and marketing but our product lagged behind. (...) Acquiring Performable enabled us to really become more of a product company - more of a West Coast-style, product-centric company." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8yihldCy9fP2_-aDgyTyv_gVY2m1HikZH1M4clJL1fRgf4K24Ka0TJ36jxkfbTo59wUKKSSWPtDsVmU_lwby0740FHMgRWGjCeIGW0cRdhXZVApTrmiERQ7Y7TK-a6j6r0ynK9_9N8fPcA6aT3nFQsrre7qjVKkTqDm0IFr41jdTm7eENvMTyln7Dto2huKjwKUnsE90qK61l-JYIH-9nJD> . 


Baking the Mobile Cookie


BlueKai is taking the wraps off a mobile extension of its core data management product. "Marketers and publishers will now be able to tap into first or third party mobile data to identify, analyze and re-target valuable mobile site visitors as well as prospecting new audiences who are on-the-go." Additionally a new Mobile Privacy Guard technology aims to calm privacy fears. Press release. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001guhT5GFre8xu6FrpIYzvaB_6AZ0B9o8r13wHn8fnBR9haPLWmD5UzKV5qUIwJJJYcFpL-aNZA3_AbIUticoJSCHgf5C9fDg52VopD5Wa4y1YlsoP3jpLN9FkPKRZca0CMfSk1ntKoCgTseooAwUubsxz61ydN47m5L5FeMJQuSQkXwDKWdhs-rgL7mXU47HtF09QaYOF4eM=>

The Addressable CMO


Forbes' Shel Israel covers last week's Salesforce Dreamforce event and says - similar to IBM and Oracle - the company is positioning to address the CMO directly with the Marketing Cloud that has Buddy Media and Radian6 at or near its center. Israel writes, "The event revealed more about Salesforce corporate strategy than Marketing Cloud product strategy, and more important, it revealed the company's perception of the state of social media in the enterprise and the evolutionary importance of marketing departments over IT in terms of technology sales." Social Ads Meet POS


It's another 'holy grail' moment for digital ads -- this one involving a pairing between Facebook and loyalty card tracker Datalogix that could help marketers follow the cookie crumbs from offline sales back to online ad views. The Financial Times hits the privacy panic button with its headline ("Facebook Raises Fears...") but the piece -- syndicated by CNN -- isn't all that inflammatory. Emily Steel writes, "Datalogix compiles a report for Facebook and its advertisers to measure which creative approaches and demographic targeting persuade people to buy specific products offline." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ImACt_zPD3EhDTOH2YHPSTJHnxOBhpZg7z9mnVdFI0xQYBXmmQMvxeEXsrroemdDtPSaalgDqaAJVxiHbB_aTBoESVdN--k5CGxqxPEjk0j0XOAAYKpGWglID3G2ozG-DDebJfKEpUa2SmkBlmigHKLYjWdEFWAWF2fEGhNGEc0EwnfXExkClA==>  CNET reports <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ImACt_zPD3FLdxSJjWrLeQupxM1LQP70rdXtKzsT3hCO1hTk-3antnktZSDx1khRyI9bt5XzpC4wSCrIc8uzI2CrY4HzML2GlJvO--uYTICJye4GobI7qwe9HPpz6B-mtoak13xTyoqebXffoGXWhmPFD6habbV84qYMlqmt4OHvlEktV70lzn2wOH2zk-M6BBoLFiVwAhWJ7Eo2jBG99oty_cOiA9zI>  privacy advocates want the FTC to step in. GOOG Research


In a note to investors, Citi analyst Mark Mahaney raised his stock price target for Google stock to $850 (yesterday, at market close, it reached an all-time high of $749 <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ImACt_zPD3EqWESTbIITzVT-pY3xGqSJuIzhBdA9T1qyk2v8pnj4I5PHXYbuMU2llhouWMfVMEjYrWNlhS4sewg05JsCY7Q6ekUHCEFCNKF32Xe0vHyNpbW_Cb6-R1iYPcR8B3Ntn90HBdPFGAeVLebnyES-gl1TtbcafloxjKQ=> ). Among the positives he sees for Google in the next 12 months are Product Listings Ads (PLAs), essentially search ads with rich product information. "We are already seeing early evidence of a) retailer adoption - e.g. 60%+ of ChannelAdvisor clients plan to participate - and b) superior performance - 2X-3X conversion rates vs. text Search ads. PLA could materially impact Q4 results."


eXelate Takes $12M


Analytics is still commanding venture capitalists' attention, so it should be no surprise that the continued competition in the space has connected data provider eXelate with the money men again. The company has raised $12 million, bringing its total VC haul to $32 million since opening its doors in 2007, AdAge's Jason Del Rey reports. The money could be used to purchase other analytics companies, CEO Mark Zagorski tells the magazine. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ImACt_zPD3FS8YzJu8RFfmAzxiCDeHrrFFMLMVKLrpftXAEBOe5dH5KpsKL5Z8sk70N2VaDpVd_77VgEvi1hzF1aOOhF_mzhKRl0f9x0c3-uK4GkN0wgZusSWgvuo-4_qDj9FzzgdH5nthhFVhfEI6WXQUxxBISJmr78anx_WPGlDG2Sb3541WeEGupkUyK4EhHpRnM4vv64D1DLc2CscpYrga7QC6g4> . 


Specific Media 'Cleans House'


After touting itself as an entertainment network when it bought Myspace, ad network Specific Media is getting back to its ad tech roots. The company has released Householding, which it bills as an all-in-one media-planning solution that allows advertisers to reach all digitally connected devices within a multi-screen household. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001ImACt_zPD3EgOJN11CYheQbdD7_8o76gRyWhIf25WOsiN2A4JaD4eZqax3NRKdnWoOuUGX99h6Jd0KIq2FsMNs7UgVOE0IyLpsJqHl1uTifPdFf-M_Swld30Zd2VjYll43LOobNJJI4bYx1OKmmAcx5_jwda3pU1Jlmz-W4GY0t6zcBss7sldOkIh4UXbk7xLmVKu1Vnl3g=> . 


Mediaocean Gets A Rave


Matt Straz, CEO of Namely, got a preview of back-office ad buying software provider Mediaocean's new digital pre-buy application, SmartRFP, and he's found himself "both surprised and impressed" by he first major new product release of the merged Donovan and MediaBank. Writing in Mediapost, Straz praises the offering, with some caveats. "It would also be great for agencies to get more transparency into publisher pricing across account teams. Finally, a contact list of the sales reps at each publisher would also be a welcome development and eliminate the need for "Does anyone have rep contact info at publisher X?" email blasts that go out across agencies." Please Pass The Risk


Venture capital dude Jerry Neumann returns to his Reaction Wheel blog to recap some of the recent chatter on entrepreneurship and offer his own thoughts. He writes, "Here's a question to ask yourself: if you think you can double revenue next year, what's holding you back from increasing revenue by 10x? If the answer is that there's no market yet, then keep grinding away at it. If the answer is not enough people or hardware for scaling, then start spending the money on hiring them, today." Ad Tech Aspirations


On AllThingsD, Kara Swisher says that results form past acquisitions are not stopping Yahoo! from potentially going into ad tech acquistion-mode. She writes, "It's water under the bridge, apparently, since the group has been making the rounds, helped by Yahoo's M&A execs, with a wide range of companies in many different ad tech area being considered (and some dismissed), including: Mediaocean, Turn, Criteo, PubMatic and Millennial Media." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshFZjEAOw4jfb7Xa42qkk10FclMHLhg8YjVPq5QqlbFpHLMUESgwM-KgCcxdCIARLm6gqkkvH-4Sy32dEdILlBsG3dY_GxsOlxiMaWoTce4hqleKWF6sqVNrmlKnFvfS-G11EMFS9qCJPjJxPKEsNO0U6_3_OQiYEcINHrTj5SaJoi6GcKt13kBowN_D7shN9fDjLzPBMwL0mMP8TVgD9nG0ahl3v5iQRFtLNfxEN-utZ34IlXJXJzHl>  


More Mobile Funds


Mobile ad server Mopub announced late last week that it has taken in $12 million ($20 mil total) in new VC funding. VentureBeat's Jolie O'Dell writes, "MoPub will be using the new funding to make big hires in New York and San Francisco, all the better to get the attention of ad agencies and brands." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshFfoWQ6p39E09cOuhhqRZ_fhu0PZZbZJ0dGekOu7uwBWdfOApKFCCXMRRRZsJ_HdW4WXZQ9us3F0tET6f9XNUQnkzTBKQSt4OgZHuAfTVdOMh7a11doHZK0q0kLtmnFg9r-egNYHbnXyqEgh-qlMUNm> . And, read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshF7LQpFS_glfuTyqhTLnRCyYU35Av9fPRh9VoJxLdIWpPPntTklvc61P4AmjvP0tKt9BTIkUrTezuYovXxDMyNQjf0PV3CoVh4s5muO4BeLW9CekyHwmualdTBI6CdUoTnecRf0vF2NQ4wrBdYAQa2DCFgCjhfHX0ELcUPIT3EaoLtB3xoC7UDKTdRU2iN-_jDpM9DQ40CtKpkrteu9x6mb>  which, in the boilerplate, claims this differentiation: "Unlike other companies that only provide one piece of a solution, MoPub manages all of a publisher's advertising inventory needs-including direct campaigns, ad network mediation and real-time bidding-in a single product." 


Data Dystopia


French ePresse consortium GM Frédéric Filloux sees a dystopian future ahead courtesy of Facebook, social media and big data. In a post on his media/tech blog, The Monday Note, Filloux hypothesizes, "Seattle, winter 2020. In a meeting room overlooking the foggy Puget Sound, Alan Parsons, head of human resources at the Wilson, McKenzie & Whitman law firm holds his monthly review of the next important hires. Parsons is with Marcus Chen, a senior associate at Narrative Data Inc., both are poring over a selection of resumés. (...) Narrative Data doesn't track core competencies. The firm is more into character and personality analysis..." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshGb1Bi_qGMVr1s7ZTVeY_HTTjiU0iGlXnTSNwr1AMB8r2C6gHhTutEl4GfCWSb-gFM43jjQwTFVTUt5V1iQBvICS_LFsqphRvGBhSBIG2XeqN8P9Nr2S2tg8nRqrENH74p4casUnOnkdUEBJXEwb-SW8njaHXsXWtzuloRnqiGC-w==>  


Do Not Track Chant


33across and its CEO Eric Wheeler continue to be on the public warpath (see previously on TechCrunch <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshHG_OtvK_empSzhbqCyAYeU5a8k0s8zNtNS6qIQ_Aut1ZNmHWdXPjaLl-n5buKXTQGqV2VKy3SXnSVCZDSiFIZOEjWFdrtmKLOUx7XmcYkX9QvqRGqV00fnmHxRLySw5u7rf9ZwDhvDjnrvN1cTzU5Ki4XqOL6J7nB-_yh6bWqn3xFsmZVdr8OuEWqAFQvO9Sxs39BH0dqCeDEW_3zGtxDR1l6oMlfNfNOd4y7r756-xA==>  and Digiday <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshEglb5i4hS0oa_unjss1R2yAK2Ec8aRT2cs-dEL7VhP4gFetd_J7QkPIBcozXmc66SPCmZsKQ2FbPeQgRDlp73Jo6ZUnubdixNk9CuF2SYpi0xHUqj9TeaoKXWsmeMvufcKwN7MktjTyQkcYxEZ0jFFmBljtqRhYYcHuNg-hyMQBQ==> ) against Do-Not-Track legislation as the company published another anti-DNT piece - this time on CNET: "The perils of 'Do Not Track' extend well beyond the ad industry. Small publishers and startup ventures alike stand to lose the most under more stringent online restrictions. Most of these companies depend heavily on advertising to generate revenue. Not just any advertising--but interest-based advertising provided by responsible third parties committed to strict industry regulation." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshGlyJ5VjUTlmJfmGeejNQqZACAflAANAa-5trcSTJJAUM8L3ohNgBtDVEdHOJW5437KSe0bf9R06W2NQQIZuCmB1e0gWIa_LFNhoWO2PFE7i6mtH7VK6dTbQss1zLjobKgsN8lWE2xiuWojQ346TWxWyjI1iHDfHSDsqEybZO0ZQadInv91YAuhHnDTbSCycIU049fDOYaoiw==>  Wheeler is quickly establishing himself as being at the "public" front lines of the sometimes radioactive Do-Not-Track discussion - perhaps even ahead of the IAB. Former Omniture CEO and current Domo CEO Josh James tweeted <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshHOkyuqhtmXtJMsknjWSoA63_U-eZypag8a2t7O1Vi5RYOXNUq00IKeZn64UiTorCFUsWGJd5RIx6lQGmLIp0HCwEWmwjegOWoMlFh6M1vROBvDgwoozxZ6XbajDHN7omosRIL2cKQzzc7oVYAvS6Vq>  about the article: "We need to kill #DNTrack legislation or seriously curb. It's our job as industry." Lawyer Sarah Downey presented an opposing view this weekend on TechCrunch <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshH0ZaKInUQJE1AVrdp9F3GsbTYvlpkrQGnf76XISgZKgwQ2FF55hVyYBFQi7d8CTI773Ej8i1SCeBiM93sBVV3rlXQ2Iw8qrHrwndgEXufiSdJ2EkRwWLAx-qNXHoaxkLIFxAO11L0pXCDeN8dxs7e3DDP6RPpDLW9saIJccGYeWwA5E3t3CNTWq13IcK0Hcw5JvRRjLXKA_KJGyQLNVsQo> . 


The Meeker Shall Inherit


Mary Meeker, she of the annual Internet Trends report <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshEGmqxsSIfPGMRO7roi8JFgU9HVD2SDc1EgQvaNq1pPAMBuiNfLSLaSDR4xWr_sFeXS_O5R8SfduuLj_lgk-edqNDVu7-Ak4Fbg5EyAzF4TNPaHMbVirwkXakr1ljZzFYkNZ1t4mOEEcg==> , speaks to Wired about life at Kleiner Perkins. The VC firm is nothing if not hands-on. "For every company that we invest in, someone here is assigned to get to know and use the product intimately and well. But that can't be the person who leads the investment-or even the person who happens to be most passionate about the product." On the question of over-investment in tech: "Public market valuations are lower than private market valuations, and that shouldn't be the case. There will be a lot of companies that don't live up to their valuations." Read it.

Data Head, Analog Heart


Megan Fearnow writing in MediaPost offers tips on building personas "beyond the dataset." The keyword here is emotion: "A consumer's online behavior and demographics (digital shopability) may show that he wants to buy a Mercedes, but his head may be telling him to buy a minivan for the kids, and his wallet dictates he should buy an economy car." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001An1rhwBeshEoYpkBBM0wMrulIAAgJPxubIkNHdxusLf0nwn7Au6kkvJLyuR2ddfYPkhC8wG9-3wW4pNJRtpt2IhPMAJ3lDFwG65-QpE6h4oT-_QR8TkMVaUdmecISTf_VxkMyMvrZ9fJczX8RE25PkMD6BBrwJObWkjyz7pJdOczb5fxBkgh0eKqLYI0Z-P7fNLLFXlVigVLnDtaqBrmHcEFxzXaEpaDMKgjVzFdKAU=>

Facebook Ads 'Common Mistakes'


If marketers are complaining that Facebook's ad offerings don't work, it's probably because they don't fully understand how to use them. That's the nutshell from a presentation by Facebook's Gokul Rajaram, Product Director Ads, at AdExchanger's Human Centered Automation conference yesterday. Business Insider's Nicholas Carlson has the rundown. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8d07DhtioozK2388bAD8BxMxKOllO8hztaZ2hLrle24AxHJNhhpw4WdJYRfiU_sgsMSuGLxU89gbOWOCtcQbbWBSJOH_doAmnYMWnz8Dk6dAYoPCkFYIovGK-7UHqyDWp3kOiCMTJXD1P312Rn4xpozotCnvIa273xk3KPa-GV-j20C2IsSzK0tc_5XDMxWFpLOmGntNT0nX9D71VJH032WkKKC3yWOzLY=> . "Through the new Facebook Ad Exchange, marketers can target, on Facebook, users who have visited their Web page in the past. Rajaram thinks marketers don't do that enough," Carlson writes. 

AOL Magnifies Video


You can talk about "premium" and "quality" all you want, but unless it scales -- reaches enough of the targeted audience -- it won't matter at all. With that in mind, AOL, which has been hoping to derive more dollars from high production value video, is teaming up with curator Magnify to get greater distribution. "We're always looking for new ways to gain additional exposure for our content and drive advertiser value, and this partnership helps us deliver on that mission," Ran Harveno, SVP of The AOL On Network, told Techcrunch's Rip Empson. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8eIkxV2UrgfsBARj48M-ZWZeeWwaRt4WWV6O0NSNngBt8siOH8c74frORJWXpmZ5OLJxblwsxfeUQfXDccriYfj1bxwztJpPYt6dOhiXzFbPu4RARc1EY8lBGbwQLoEjxFzhZwAFxsbNdyFEhz4S37YWJ3t0GIJlGmY1YGeyLCMKAjq_6GsCkD92bWIMYQldvzSt2gA2v-oC5BfEckCutYf> . 


Social Strategery


Facebook has added a new class of Preferred Marketing Developers (PMD) for "Strategic" partners who are driving "outstanding positive impact" in the ecosystem. Who makes the cut? Twelve companies, including Adobe, Nanigans, and Brand Networks. Says the blog post, "Each Strategic PMD earned the distinction through a rigorous selection process that among other considerations, is based on shared values, strategic alignment, and growth potential with Facebook." Read more.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8fJzDNSczty02JwmGpRTclUTToQlt_XxOQCJ1Aakp5gfYCg-t0tVux-XrjDCVuV0A2YKYNsiB1N43CIAF0lfHauDvFQ-t1BzLNf_am02ZhyCXqtVvow0VTO5J9xJ5GVrUoHxtIL0tiwojedIWhdKCV73yDAy0TurgHusQb1-kxy3g==> 


New Strategic Eco-chart


Boutique I-bank LUMA Partners claims to have ripped the lid off of strategic partners in the ad tech sector in its first-ever iteration of a Strategic buyers ecosystem map. LUMA's Terence Kawaja writes, "Today we are publishing the most important industry map - the Strategic Buyer LUMAscape <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8fJ1AmFAu8ADAAAtZmZrahdeo-sFxw8YgKTCjtMRnAHagWLsDecuzR6KTfuwO6l53er_9AI96msdqlwufeqjezaT2sK4JqF7wCmrSJ7OipbzK0WBa-_lndW6UeS2ycmvPFbJtYk0E07x0gimtRdce9mZnlHKQr8hdo=> . Historically, digital acquisitions were dominated by four core companies: Google, Microsoft, Yahoo and Aol. While this group remains relevant, we have witnessed an expansion of the buyer universe as digital business models converge across media, software, services and commerce." Mobile Tracking's Larger Problem


With Apple weathering all the bad reviews for replacing the Google-powered map app that was formerly embedded in the iPhone's previous operating systems, the issue of replacing the unique identifier on its mobile devices is probably an after thought at the moment. Still, the ability to balance tracking user behavior and maintain privacy is a big issue and the alternatives to the UDID is coming. ClickZ's Matt Kapko surveys the UDID's successors. But whatever tracking tool is used, there's a larger problem facing marketers. "We need to dispel the myth that tracking is bad and evil," said Gareth Davies, commercial operations director at Somo Global. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8ezld4vJriZdZYJPkDo_sR86xhsjNH9jUX_eoHbgBU9at8ckKAC30jjHGryOB0lleHyUE7IJqSdXc_037EW5pxxAsbhOfHSZkdA2P2XkOthEdUXd3_MFxdyaYJayNRtdcYWCYVf7ULiRlVRMIt2bKWcRzpbCRsH8hsDz6PFdFEuX4ik_lBBEYuG7uedzTQnlZ7n7atd11zxpmXHA516Fl0Kunu7hdc9JTo=> .

Data's Social Value


Instead of trying to ply their users with more ads, perhaps social networks should spend more time trying to derive value from their data directly. That's the view of IBM Collaboration Solution's social analytics strategist Marie Wallace, who tells O'Reilly Radar's Ron Miller, "The key is that in most cases ads only work in a search-like context, however with most social media sites people are not going there to search. They are going to converse with friends and family, which makes ads interruptive and frequently invasive." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8eayiXcuwIc9WmNe59WYSWZCSt0sgUSF_yZ7PSrtTLZPpIy5sHwonk7pof56RSbSgKdbxXCJZqi6v_5vlE4KCdDKofVo9rHv_J9ZEE2V06HlOqW9xPUW3FtVUMg_mkiLZv_JSHAG9NwIejn1xoN0ScP5FIqRxZZ_FY=> . 


Data Pinning


As the industry evaluates Facebook's and Twitter's marketing options, the ad industry is turning its expectations to image-sharing site Pinterest. Ad tracker Convertro has had some preliminary talks about revenue-generating ideas with Pinterest, Adweek's Tim Peterson reports. Convertro CEO Jeff Zwelling shared some of the ideas, all of which are anchored to Pinterests immense, real-time flow of data and shows obvious purchase intent. "If someone keeps repinning Marc Jacobs dresses, there's a high probability they want to buy Marc Jacobs dresses," Zwelling observes. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001N2KfxO_NO8eIkxV2UrgfsBARj48M-ZWZeeWwaRt4WWV6O0NSNngBt8siOH8c74frORJWXpmZ5OLJxblwsxfeUQfXDccriYfj1bxwztJpPYt6dOhiXzFbPu4RARc1EY8lBGbwQLoEjxFzhZwAFxsbNdyFEhz4S37YWJ3t0GIJlGmY1YGeyLCMKAjq_6GsCkD92bWIMYQldvzSt2gA2v-oC5BfEckCutYf> .

Google Crowned Display King


Google has been battling Facebook for dominance of the total display ad market for over year, ever since Yahoo was ousted by the two after a long reign. Now, eMarketer is ready to declare a winner for 2012, saying the search giant will earn more U.S. display advertising revenues than any other company, topping the market with a 15.4 percent share, according to eMarketer. "There are several factors underpinning Google's ascent to market leader, including the continued strength of its ad network, video advertising on YouTube and mobile display advertising on AdMob," eMarketer says, adding that Facebook's slight revenue shortfall ahead of its IPO was also a cause. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davox090k-i7knF3j10AB6VLO6HuwjXFNiaZWKKnIiZwTYva2zushGHGcHRtZxbTwEDB1qpZyRytvabcRermXSfwjQoTc88vksjOfnIonPPdDYE5sOW_MG9_zbwAw56pmDAiEsvdeNqblEO3YFfcB5wRTT> . 


Ford's Digital Wish? Straight Talk


What's the biggest obstacle holding back brand dollars online? Simple confusion, says Ford CMO Jim Farley in an interview with Digiday's Brian Morrissey. "Digital for most marketers is very intimidating. Your media partner has to hold your hand." He recalls fondly one media rep who told him his ad was wretched. "I will never forget that person saying my ad was wrong. He said, 'I got your money, but you're making a mistake.' I wish that would happen more regularly in digital." Read the Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davow2JaARCAI7jS8tKfxpjxVcMTDudn8wlGb7zeoiU3QO_WbG50SexQ6CBizVLHdlerVJKvOnDT7v_ov6C1X5janCJpTDwmarE97Dgo9YYjvXsLKiT7i0PDCvA8bqMknZmA0ABczPhGd4Wn1pmUpIo3t1rcRw25dEhtje0HrDIRi0mA==> &A. 


Opening China


Display ad platform OpenX is continuing to build up its position in Japan and is using the country as a launch pad for a planned China expansion, ClickZ's Adaline Lau reports. "Whether it's Japan or across Asia, we are deeply committed to the region," Jason Fairchild, OpenX's chief revenue officer, says. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoweJIZqplmI-4YiDT-IXn14CDO87jg2inZTjn5la2sPNBBj7XTaPrR2KQLy0RJZb3Fz0hIbzSB3LEaZSRFCsnCwOIjCm4_Xzy3D3-uWBAUG8ekBx3NoeJqxKGYxStEKftaTXUPMzWSpmbyvqZcl4M5xOF7FcwUXqzSWYr47WjYIkSfGx6oFKgmykS2PkcNaRaaMroZF7MP89g==> . 


Striking Back At Patent Trolls


Cloud computing provider Rackspace says its been hit with another patent lawsuit, simply for hosting a site called GitHub. Rackspace is going on the offensive, calling out its attackers, PersonalWeb Technologies, as patent trolls, Alan Schoenbaum, Rackspace's general counsel says in a blog post. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoy-ahlcDGcy9ANaANYJ7FlAfaWzB18zfKTKiqZa2Dk8SwKcopHI8ik-lt0G_hRz53nfzGSJ89s-1apmvGhqM9FhkaZ-l5jahX2KZVCBqrfwoTch3wF8moDwKU8JsnoPhN-QqjH9_8MGunhXsnWdcgvBE1CgZP9zNwM=> . "It's apparent that the people filing the suit don't understand the technology or the products enough to realize that Rackspace Cloud Servers and GitHub are completely different products from different companies," he writes. 


Collective Decision


Ad tech firm Collective is ordering its company-wide sales team to get certified by the Interactive Advertising Bureau. Certification requirements including an exam (get your application here <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoz9hxsgHfgVp6g4-3UsLzHPrAZ7zpRsC459hCrE_myYDQDwNCZKBIYPxin53Ld6E736um1OyOs0DEOH9OOKjK2BIPuzpj7jGbfcym0cXIsnwebjo-p4q_Qv>  if you dare). "The interactive landscape is too competitive-and too complex-not to make sure that your executives are fully equipped with the intricate knowledge base and skill sets they need in order to thrive," explained Jed Savage, EVP, Media Sales and Strategy, Collective. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoyPlSkxhbci2k4jaHwVk4RFZhNLO8YDmFl-FZLGcxHSSs2ZUGvwYvfILkKIOpec6bAj90D3x5m1eHaqBuk2b2zSl-mWZxQw6_H0EnNLJu4K3YgIMEmXuJs09RTdlakjbz496Gh-YIAmTBPU_ondv0o0nBHHj-X8PmHBomiRLqcWO0_S02KJXiwjMe-qoxa3mVlp6tvzfFj1UE-y4kot3KQU> .

Nielsen's eGRP Posse


Nielsen has saddled up a bunch of ad platforms to support its Online Campaign Ratings product, which offers apples-to-apples measurement for cross-media advertising. Turn, DataXu, FreeWheel, and Audience Science are among the 15 new "pardners" equipped for the high noon showdown in measurement town. Press release. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoytPNL3SwTjWEz1mOXbZt3lEAEIR0ucNTRDcMmZjp52ESvdr5TwmYDsuYyXBlXEi6iG_LGGhJGu4c-hPBkgfXZxgKYunYDrqpIL2RFUnUoeUWHiLDenVOgWOUoQQ75xl3OIpMj5g0taMYAIgB1bp8PTmDFcrxNSaqiXnCdR_Mnm8N0MFJP6tXxOgd-GQ1U6XnGQSRKOZV5Hnrq5OWePCtmRX6JkcLhtI4Ma_BubzqqQv_6ujJBVPhvvl5U482Om7DWBRKeNsrXRLA==>  


DoubleClick Updates


When DoubleClick announced its unified stack back in June (i.e. the Digital Marketing Manager), it was really announcing its plans for the coming one to two years. Much of the integration work still lay ahead of it. Well, now it's begun in earnest according to a post on the DoubleClick Advertising blog. For example, the re-built bid manager of Invite Media is in working order ad Google claims, "Customers using the new Bid Manager to target, optimize, and buy display media have seen improved performance, including seeing 16% more inventory due to infrastructure improvements that reduce our latency with exchanges." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoxPvLEKTc6QJMl3UFF7bUng81FRh4bzPLeMWFmPjw1YKpiyUSB-_yIqFHoYLNH5aUXwkYxi6mEkCjjuQwsh-O1qnH_SxrUHwHBy6CaEeVYB2-dj-d6CL-5fF2yP6PuGbf8g9jiGBceY479_KFomWKjFE5Cz6mdt_dnfCff0qRN5viU-ZBDWnkfahLRJYdcGU3Q=>  


Enter 'Salesforce Marketing Cloud'


Salesforce unveiled the first fruits of its Buddy Media and Radian6 acquisitions -- called the Salesforce Marketing Cloud -- at its Dreamforce conference. Unilever's VP, global media innovation, Babs Rangaiah, likes it: "Unilever has fully embraced this social transformation and a partner like Buddy Media, now Salesforce Marketing Cloud, empowers us to scale our social programs globally and across many brands. This is incredibly valuable," he says in a canned statement. Press release.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001p2fDN7davoz4Ea5-8i0ZgP8lV60yYyzUwEmB5IgMbLaJbY0NDRQglr7rhTxr8AabrReBQuXnhMVI2DGIgtPsMyShN2aWfEaDrx_Qgbp88JwrR-CN4mFbOHs-SVwBkuDWbri53Fov0T4rAnl3Aev5gt5bbF87U94naPltt_W3AiSKJHZci7NAvediMF2b76VIlgZ5NBHwrPA=>

Yahoo's Alibaba Cash


Alibaba's long-time-coming share repurchase from Yahoo has come to pass, and Yahoo investors are to be the main beneficiaries. Wall Street liked the payout (YHOO is up nearly 2% after hours), but is doing right by shareholders the wrong thing for Right Media? The liquidation move puts to rest speculation that Yahoo would hoard much of the cash for reinvestment in its ad exchange and other technologies. It will still keep some, CEO Marissa Mayer said in a statement: "This yields a substantial return for investors while retaining a meaningful amount of capital within the company to invest in future growth." More coverage in WSJ <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvlDVOYkWlAdTZ8lQ6nC3eKneIiaaBSsvWtx7BodXe4Lj-88HGpSoOPwBRX3MLoGqzMBrLRpaEOAXRwfp9QZkPp8qMYXFzVx2xzB8BPb8mrRPOEExporJ1xj4bL7GzXweJU64JlF6a8Y859_ibxySwRftsmp_J1zkx9vQnL0bLRbgw0ZnG4V4xes>  (registation), Business Insider <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvnQZpLCQOtKu9ajoeGjaIbfnI9WHgBfiDDjGQnZWKGO573YRYhVTAAgkfj8SI3wRC6gysoIw62rTBoYjGe_mU9Ys7j6OHuG8eQyRDqlzGjtAcNPmMfHMfOZT61Y1X4QDqHf8aJ30I_CfrRkeoMmYXCaNtZeLTTLZ8GvetYzP_qhNQ==> , Bloomberg <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvmP0Sv8JAVYFa9vBKgdPIRJeVdel-UaFhDJWfAVHYS6zpqE_VlNQrCW7jd9OtnxEj9-ei0AegXJvcaakHOHYJTJzjxBWowSto3de4JLmDBh9lwfmwlf4tpafh9uN9LdGb9auX_VgrtB-BbjaqoQCe37zXzDTjQYUje_hZT7JB_G4t_Ab9fX_QVY81K3aGRH8Tdd36PuGju7GzEM4Ed4tTwtgpwaVcBb3ag=> , and AllThingsD <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvkYfta62PANmSHtVsDwYJS6Zsz96F4bPhIAuiB-Rq9lv1pKDroLjRF_JJjKB_w6765n35FUDllOB9ahirwrmGeu9NOLVk5HBKyAmU72wy_j9DBUzlRVZCWB64Ch2zqVV68vBknBb3jomwNTAlb8XvIgzQc_4IIu3n2Uk5rBqNB4MA==> . 


Pledging Mobile


Kraft will up its mobile spend to 10 percent, Kraft media director Melissa Laux told the audience at a Mobile Marketer event in NYC. Gartner Research VP Mike McGuire, who caught her presentation, says, "While a total figure was not disclosed...Laux made clear they were pulling the budget dollars from TV, print, out-of-home and digital."
Read McGuire's post. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvncDXdZCSALZ7H9mOnHjFIaYr2YoSjz6zmVzKXTmUgVZCIZskO3xRoAbSU8QDSqNscU6X0N4YMoEQ6Om4Kz8cq9eaXwXQWTvYc6ZKo1T6sV8nsBI_Nnm3L7t8z4u2ICP2hB-o9HlESunGwvDMs2bOZng1QogzWnsJCRtFM85Mq_r7mCMBFyCtl61gxiqJdgGIKteOZHPg7xPBYvQz1JM1srfZCOeeJ0X3wwFP4Ci0c6KPpnm5qBl3VY>  Meanwhile ClickZ's Adaline Lau reports Reckitt Benckiser is also upping its mobile commitment. More. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvkI7TRsklb0whPSdeadomBscX-yadqFZD_ycUwsxnfxq5dpF-B-eXHCpHLuUC-a7fn-1XA3ntouEX0U1c-yBPlytsiqk3P5E5Sk77YG-9GNPWw1UH27Ef9bTBiyOGzqgi8RGYsWCadldgefqSlU6_zG-eq7hcE327woDa1_y3yIjUO9F-1Wv7vGXYcr8mrXPZ-A5HRdf9jNJ9S39imc272->  


Vivaki AOD Gets GM


Five months after its previous general manager Kurt Unkel climbed the ranks to lead Vivaki Nerve Center (AdExchanger interview <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvk5N9ageikp6jjOIAsf1Zya1n0O9RYdy6AGkLyIT1FZsfSSHmbcAuH2_wc-iNsv5X86ZQyzmN4aEyYDi_UDIqCmiOx0jHll8Oa6X8qu3GTOKvUJTbAtXgQIoqDrLpD_KdZ_HOt-2NlsYiR7PXgaaHs2J7gbeNzSEf8=> ), Vivaki's AOD unit has slotted in a new guy to oversee the day-to-day at the trading desk. Chris Paul was previously at Digitas leading the AmEx media team. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvn2OaDCMDkKl5kzCG_UFt9UB6FG9Yz2VIgPYP4Lg14Q_yXb3xk_oALEWqvbBExH_gi52cNQe58hDtm1jPp9jU7w5d47d-P2q3-NdtpKbHFs5UzZa1CVMzwnR_un-C9deB6vK9ZAFyQNUsmqgvlMJrqRZGc-ooYPS-EiIZkSyR4yt3fZhw5dUKLshybWlNNb4iIH97joHZMcE_-Ev2Hq3OJ_2Lh76lt_mkywOtbeMuibOoylGPWnGRd3SWkW9qmd2peGY_bHpB5bJQ==>  Separate but related: Adam Shlachter, formerly of MEC, has joined Digitas as SVP Media in New York. He replaces Paul on the AmEx business. More on that. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvmJA4Zvkx6pQfjLJ1egZGJBbQmFfev8RfCVyHmnE5cj-021NjUhNaQLXFPp-UtvptxVSuBZKgzrdo-_jpEwfENjk8uumOCb7S-wToJbvSJjetGW8oInqTTj9gVnPOVt_cKJ38WQgjExwAFomimbdCHXOGUtGFxnYEnsM9AliV6jOiMqDWlkEGt_iPskXgRbdV8=>  


Social CRM Siren Call


Dreaming about social CRM? Dream on, says Adobe Digital Marketing product guy Lawrence Mak in a post on the company's Digital Marketing blog. "There is a dif­fer­ence between the data you get from a data­base and the insights you can draw from actual cus­tomer behav­ior... Behav­ioral data is much more indica­tive of true busi­ness impact and influ­ence than pro­file data," Mak writes. His advice: ask social CRM vendors the tough questions. Read it.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvltuOYb1mszjO-rXk96L-xgjg4W5Bqv3P9JlSR-7UMg5Ids_T4_rMhqZSsXZsr_XHu6RRqh7HEYKiwSnmZT8rPuq_pqSAKCg2ILQjNYy2gaB4673EflwSZKdw4stSUGS7aICE_nQmc8B7vq3dy5KrV3gFNvDEZGuvWwCumYyiUCyGNyqPjXpJDZtlSDFaK6Z3owJWPjoBhLAOwZfhjtZAWW> 


Visualizing Audience


Optimal is making its keyword visualization tool available to everyone. The idea is to expose a "visual web" of relationships for topics on Facebook, which in turn is meant to spark new audience buying possibilities on the social platform. To see a sample web of keywords in the auto sector, click here. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvlQjKAJJUdDtKigELqpOrSuuQDZq9F3ECE5IKxSFksvPvkfRX3TjUqR_8QC5RvxwD-dgQM6M49Z_O0w_5WRR_1dQ0b1y3Co3-ka0-yKksAxcgYB8HKBxiA6AxggY5M0RqwTgkUZgOY3pfUGZ6mRvYoJl2l0HkjVgBWKRFIVoS_yTLsfOnxx68mC>

Agency Automation


Forrester analyst Joanna O'Connell, like just about everyone in the ad business, it trying to figure out just what the media agency of the future will look like as programmatic buying becomes more mainstream. (She'll be speaking about the issue at AdExchanger's Human Centered Automation <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvn69AVSpgaysv3pCxW_keKqh_2OKd5gw5rCgYDCeZIcAOScq9c2-NFNwJdppRe0lCasVC5trOb-7f97Ygg_BvAuqMGn7ATGuq7-Zao8nvsTc982pfcEvGjhVKIkJriz4d8=>  conference this Thursday.) She tells Digiday's Brian Morrissey that the agencies will be bifurcated between analytics and strategy. She also sees trading desks becoming extinct. "The idea that media would be managed by some removed group at the holding company rather than the team that works with the client: I don't fundamentally think that has a future," she says. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvkv7xsEgmg53uaeyte8uHrwmd-hbqIHHw3ooOlP2u6j4MjwQ-fEmEdFbUtHskJzz9XyFmqP1YGaBE60dQFHf0UTN8LoZRQhD9KzRJmxc2VkAzDOkOQl4nU5_zJT5vq7lnO7O8uZdCZknseZJhJXIGpJH04Ed7DJd64=> . 


The 'App' in AppNexus


AppNexus is once again using its blog to drive awareness of its app strategy. A new series of posts takes up where its "30 apps in 30 days <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvlYZJNCwm91AxWWBaDD43yrGtrkWV8wF-krJUkJhsRgWS6mDrU0tO1sgKQeRGXJ1tRpmysKcBFbCbR0H9HVy7j_GY7ODK45FFZJHyYJWl8UuWl0rquwWOvamqBvTBpNQxwQ6ZOHZCMXTA==> " drive left off. First up is an app called Adgent Digital +Video, made for publishers that are "looking to run video advertising but don't have video-compatible inventory." Read about it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvkqDXaPfsuNtdMgsjN71KU8BsuOYaE2j5meVmSMoSQZcqo10yfrB4X7FVBePmAJlM4YAErsiNtngU4PNl_C7owM6UUlIfr8bJw2P0Vgt5kRh_TR-thhpzpmQxUnb3mDgbO8xKy5hKPLgwDVDsC_JpAb>  Seven more to follow. 


Bizo's B2B Moves


Bizo is trying to make email marketing a bit more attractive by combining it with retargeting tools. It introduced its CRM Retargeting tool, which will be rolled out fully over the next few months. "The future of online marketing is one where website, display, search, CRM, social and email lead nurturing programs are all integrated and automated, and marketers measure true attribution and ROI back to individual prospects in the CRM database," said Bizo CEO Russell Glass. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001flFi_hUfVvlisDGxge6QAtMb_5tI7TGSvJUDH6qZ4y-fli5v6U4Ro3_R-7HiX8VmqQtVo17eJnW-U1755Ym944_B-tKkmfDMFnAUPbAD4UvCp4hIWzjpKFlCxQuhyKJteBXEtJu3IbzeAdCr3weA3HulZ5nTBHPYf0QUS3ia2jszjWm_cUhImeBlFURXHlk4n1xUtWRc50CcLPc1ZsZOkXCrD4AP7HU4iGvxX884trvLQ149fJCmao-o-hO79YKLG4iSejqs8Ck=> .

Screen Size Matters


It makes sense that the more screen space you have, the opportunities for bolder creative and less clutter are more pronounced. Video ad platform YuMe collaborated with IPG Media Labs to find out just how much of a difference screen size makes -- and found that size isn't everything. "Consumer attention is fragmented across screens amid a dizzying array of content, and viewing habits differ by time of day. This year's study takes these factors into account and finds that clutter-free ad environments give advertisers the greatest ROI, regardless of screen size," Ed Haslam, YuMe's SVP of marketing, said. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lbzgLwfpFzBJ-Bife-8ZTNRnynS84tUOjjc-Bz6I4sdYCEnWCbP7bZdFc1GmxJhqgotzmsQkYwDQ-UOWvXuY9JMnk8SqsrYrRRw5QjCDbo4tpJXL7-fOul1w0CMOG8gvOHS1GRjerllDKxykQ1fWdCl3nJG4srW292lWEcWvR-bsDkB8YHRMxUH5200_ETV5O0Ho-7Oi2pCdPP5sxlRWwAP52TYm43vT68q7wv2swSTnauGusINq3ORr_qMSYPfAyhO37KhhsssnQ==> . 


Google+'s Meaningless Milestone?


As part of Google's welcome to its latest acquisition, photo app maker Nik Software, Google+, the search giant's social network answer to Facebook, says it now has 400 million registered users and 100 million monthly active users. Read the blog post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lYVYZ1ZKxM1XdwLg1mtGQw4tOcCqpIxggJU5UVdMNutD7Rxp5Jdpcm2lmtE08_cVkbx5M3iTR50LOeKSS0Nr6VkxZfuPcE_hcePRSSjO2oBXGfm8kgjmukQz3HYhjmJxgA5mRbUEBIf6e2NGLfDiuGbUCclo2ljVgQ=> . As The Next Web's Emil Protalinski notes <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lZwRl3OCjS6cwdBn6YNchatovPBP4aATUSWGhZ5ajkBtCTXFHZSV17iRq9FTeFZgmxqp4OQDqOMx3Cpb9hWlhGDqUGSV1jeGf6KAdQWk4l_jcqIZh7zwv-2DhVEpS4zAcnMQg8FMkoj7UZiQ22AZk2E7fi0rlv7vZBCN9bPESSxdXLTW4AOw283_84OHt6_M_MGeM6UsWSk_r3kmnFz59DHWxa4ikyOjzEYmKlQFN2A6VisryS6eJg5> , the most important number is the latter one - and with Facebook having passed 955 million active users this summer, Google+ still looks like an also ran. Still, having 400 million registered user may just be enough of an achievement for Google+; after all, as long as those users stay logged in, it's still pretty easy to track their web movements, whether or not they post or view anything on the social net. 


Data-Driven Commerce


Fresh from its acquisition of of retargeter MediaForge two weeks ago for its Rakuten LinkShare subsidiary, Japanese ecommerce company Rakuten has made an investment in Daily Candy-esque "Daily Grommet." AllThingsD's Kara Swisher explains, "Both Daily Grommet and Rakuten have focused on linking small and medium retailers directly with consumers, using discovery and social tools and large marketplaces. Daily Grommet was already working with Rakuten's U.S.-based Buy.com site." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lYUpjigtwqpjiHGEvD4g6kmR0v_yCXGz80nocHe4KOM8tYCvLw5GUVAMinDTOweC341CCn2pdEUhZTO31ApbU0VmGBQ2WVOtX3kK_8M-0skwMMmLfrRPraXBuiy1Dm_t_eXdc4vUJ-iC9wKPnaz6daSsZAKp00qMVRsOABb9fBc7kKu9fadKGtIGYzb3WKEJ3U2nGq4YhNQKUsNc6fday64IiFEUACp0kggn2nx_8Mkc5q9-wzVFMPI>  Rakuten, 10,000 employees strong, is steadily tying together data-driven, ecommerce business. 


Self-Serve Rant


Arnie Gullov-Singh, formerly of Ad.ly and Fox Audience Network, now of AdKnowledge, notes a self-serve platform "trip wire." He writes on his personal blog, "Having built 3 self serve ad platforms (at Overture, Fox and Adly) and been a customer of over 50 others (yes there are over 50 self serve ad platforms), the one issue that seems to arise in the lifecycle of every new cost per click ad platform is that of the minimum cost-per-click bid." Read why he thinks this is w-r-o-n-g <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-larctTkKKadc4_bAdx7LC63u3CsquN3hEo4Txx0cas9quuJI-TVp9hiXH3kkUWqH7C3Dt7Q3oambJbrbLtv6OnLD8i7Ed5IqiSwMUmHWe9N8ibcJCLeW2G0Zgp6m4DcPjir2Iib3qhM6FxsFuBybowlKuGO69r21CrvnklDPlEtK7vGmaB5JI6UkWSvA2bblrITFKBuSFnplw==> . 


Pepsi Startup Challenge


The soft-drink maker is cozying up to the Silicon Valley set, offering marketing advice to startups and hoping some tech savvy qualities are imparted to it, in return, AdAge's Natalie Zmuda reports. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lZcga8odOonnlC7lp_8B7InQbYRDLW1CK0wMJj2UZbMrcHXyPaq_BZPWjk8-zncPKrPi7O2hi_v0-5YEdS50o-IG8jZ4dR5i_2VBb8cj6vpWh27DG4bttUvs-hpVFH1zeUiZPAo0sK4-mS1a_OMtRnEiGWigS3Az-FsM0jDwlin_WirLN1jwR4PyEQJ760nSjl7JUwwA3F4ICkgjMHDSeC2pMFJrnyVCbbsSYRfzHdMMONNlRC052QSgWZtK5jYdJq6oWVuaTSdg-Kq5eNd3HM8NbjRi8SbxCu8B4j2i0B0kyWWaDpGIWEUAyy4DBRjfjPHwlupLiq23IMTNYdvphoGJsasTqFrsdxrLtKF8_nzCg==> . Pepsi is touting its role as a tech funder and incubator with its Digital Labs project, as it looks to augment the 10 percent of its ad budget spent on startups. "[Digital Labs] grew out of this need to not always rely on agencies or partners to bring us ideas or introductions to not just startups but to a lot of the disruptive marketing products that are reaching consumers," said Andrea Harrison, director of digital engagement at PepsiCo.

Paid, Owned and Earned


Nielsen share some nice data and graphics on media biz including what consumers trust most and least when it comes to ad messaging. In the study, no surprise - recommendations from a friend are most trusted. But on the least trusted side of things- mobile text ads. Who knew? Display ads on mobile and PC finished second and third from the bottom, respectively. See it now. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-laqUXauKIY5kXvyG9367eJPw_0DJXsDnSyJLU-WX3zE2DXPJyuhk3-I6xrNSDTHLnOBSE_Gc7BGIspO-Wb4D0irL9D-4V5P5-q7n1lUJJvVnS4uJRpcZovazC4T1veKuTWZS1qoakT3c9-6jxzxGMIlQvSTlPRvViTsMG6WKN2zcNER7pp79cHMXW5zRz9kXNB04hDvnXtJKEAKSjjFGHYTMIEqFn7SvUk=>  


Attribution Chasm


On Econsultancy, Encore Media Metrics CEO Steve Latham reviews whether attribution analytics are crossing into the mainstream of marketing tools and requirements. He writes, "Given that the year is now 2/3 over, I am not holding my breath for rapid transformation in 2012. But there are many positive signs, fueled in part by Big Data fever that has everyone atwitter. Mass adoption will happen when advertisers start demanding better metrics, deeper insights and demonstrable improvement in ROI from their agencies." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=0018w2llx64-lbNon_CkevHWGw4DsbIlwoOER2shEHgrUEWd-3ivE7gO2BhL4OmmCjJK3nUON3zTXMdX2_Sg7MgcuNd1-N3m-BX9o3Er-Uf7SSfDvwlckfbTFj5ekp33z0RsQcV9dygT3wkAPcP046iNLzZ1hCpTrV7d-STNEawPnFwzqPhPVy5MVX0wlprq6JZGig3MjpdBi1ELutwaexchHW7P34M4Xdh>

Buzzfeed Acquihiring


Buzzfeed acquired one-year old Kingfish Labs last week. ClickZ's Susan Kuchinskas says, "The publisher will use Kingfish's technology to enhance its ability to target Sponsored Stories on Facebook." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0ozf8BN4awP4QP7FbDBJmZ9MohSkqCK_Nf6tzrDg0F4VFCCcKN8Yu72sQIvhB_RyPLym0XdnqwwHg0JcuXwc2p-pLPWkD_LPtpTbBI8UMbTY3HGtScYQDP3XvOFIiDYw1mxIEi3cgWgs3l-QZTWgELhKjBefb4D-fF_dcTmK3_Isjr9bXwDSTEOqu8F_Ejy45Nnb4X4jrIRDw==>  GigaOm reports <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0pPduOCQvdH_NXlA-rk_KbvqDc7z85tlPIifZGcTW92Ynq0FZwkz-mjrt0K6zhCihZ857sk7zCy1dFpo8td_xJl9p-33fSKLMgTlMeKXvZGsWlemKkswNFK2ZE1mDpqSpabocn1Zu9CXnU9-hFpCGDDy6JxTXR0P-T_oNUjLgqXjin1csIjQBN9TlUe49o3WEzYcdhjYV9ThQ==>  that Buzzfeed will add three to its engineering team. No terms of the deal were made available, but the founders of both companies know each other from their HuffPo days. Kingfish had originally started with a "dating" app but then started focusing on making sponsored story campaigns work better. Charlie Wuerzel explains in Adweek <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0oxEC4epwERTqpBYSr9ADrfezcAnImW8CYGQMRKhwtoKkVgCF3Oa09GHpmioq9XrG2J2gxTTxDsr6ecQ_4EkENOKqAC5ckaMA0soHI1UOiX-JOYxNar-UrSeaBUg8MEPfOhTXGN1ylUYvvr9h48z--SOarhZokkh9m99PO09S4DS4l_AygkXkNwOBzdAfeE5yt6kv2mMZiBuQ==> . 


Programmatic dmexco


CMO.com reviews last week's dmexco show in Cologne, Germany. CMO.com's Mike Nutley says that ad automation was a hot topic. He quotes a range of industry luminaries who were present at the event including IAB CEO Randall Rothenberg who argued "that if programmatic trading grows as people expect it to, targeting and segmentation technology will become a commodity, available to everyone. 'What won't become a commodity will be creativity and strategy, and they will be what differentiates your offering,' he said." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0pDWuwoF8UMlkD0AIPRI9wfu_WCvoVBS1GiSKVYyzvXdJyBP4ZGuC5f3MV4Xo5GYSFk5jAL-8DmPErb2pkDBL8JtkkgYRlA6FGgdfILk6na95Ru4OWeJ8cDm6qZ_MxoISFirUiWba6HPPHxDDEBgf6z_MtX0PXZF1XbuUBNwzKl0ZaLAfT-IdU56zaZ3Z2gdJ0fIH9KTqjtkg==> . 


Retargeting Conversation


Lijit's Walter Knapp extends his sell-side platform/network thinking and imbibes the Federated Media kool-aid in an opinion piece on iMedia Connection. Knapp writes, "... an urban-style author writing and producing video content about a new electric car designed for city dwellers. The content is authentic, detailed on topics the audience finds interesting, informational and entertaining. The campaign content is amplified over social media and shared among publishers through related content suggestions and interactive display ads." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0oa90XY0tIe-PNnPQnyt7aekaoERt1at4rLJOCPVq7x54wOBV8VvoFsg_4RLPJ7C6zCB3e8sSNEuzQsYnneILKTHtqqZu60uyCrnD_XsfL4eA_mFPSYRUUQVozjGjjqRWPVx5Sw8iHpE6mJUGS_2PVUSTFWXzUZ_tCqSZhpRGRy97S_dVCh-MBR4UQL91szvS8=>  


Mobile Display Woes


Mobile advertising performance went under the microscope in a Sunday NY Times article. Christine Chen of Goodby Silverstein & Partners tells the NYT, "'What makes Web ads so attractive to advertisers is the ability to track actions and optimize accordingly," Ms. Chen says. Because a smartphone cannot use the same technology, she says, 'your ability to track and optimize is much more blunt, or in some cases nonexistent.'These limitations depress demand for smartphone ads and lead to low prices." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0o7EYOBinrhBIugyt10UNp23kg0vU7Afeq-iP_vs0l_9tqwhC80ApQH1WNh68FOTGk4LhMKhaR1CY_VpZM1QcIB4oPk8HEroOLasSEcbKqN7EUkx-zDzOffZyiD9GI_xBk462xCB4Stu3IjadQ6BJ1tRQ8bMCuzj0ZOm8hSlq-xtsr8Gh8O8LEf4XZKJiRALZJ14hvouvC2uG9fW_zXhyw3>  


Microsoft of the Future


In a Q&A in the Seattle Times, Microsoft CEO Steve Ballmer says that five to ten years from now, his company will no longer be just a tech company. "I think when you look forward, our core capability will be software, (but) you'll probably think of us more as a devices-and-services company. Which is a little different. Software powers devices and software powers these cloud services, but it's a different form of delivery." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0o6__Ta3TJvqvPFviVr47fIYNacdoWDOUgKOo-0ambu2lKvhlm6bDHfU9fVxVkIsTxzku--c0J0NJF-MD7hFWw8Y8JNTAhH-6zHbODgOaF56RSShDX7qSq_uo0EdkKuv7WO24Q-zXlXx_xvcYT4Pl9JEKmVkm7NBkXkvaMPADMi_eFnU13KXKQREV1edMxels8=>

Microsoft: The Agency

Microsoft is opening an agency in San Francisco reports Ad Age's Cotton Delo. Are IPG and WPP Group in the competitive set (again)? Delo writes, "Microsoft seems to be taking a unique approach with its clients. Google's efforts have been more on the agency side with its 'Creative Sandbox,' a resource for agency creatives to learn about Google products such as Android and YouTube through events and publications. With Studio 415, Microsoft looks to be bypassing agencies and going straight to brands." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001U9RIh_6Nq0o7jfz2Z0ahM4wDnT5uv7AS-M6xeYIu4nsCq1D3nrifUcQlAo-9vgl1jIizgY7d7zv46F56lWv_1EAIg7vEzETldLsi3cdGLZtDjST28Ys_wDo89_0bnBSs4LMLA0YQcM_FKx04fVBmdG4UOObXnzwjrcKKMY-3m50MigeFpjsnKAe_CyhtG129ckMDMYaBxo_eWxfU89K7IA==> .

AppNexus' European Call


Exchange provider AppNexus is the new Europeon ad platform for telecom company Orange. In March 2010, Orange had hooked up with OpenX <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0kpJ95FYIwDPpgWkFUdFYjGm8ffrqkRYfX76P4PrMFc4WYNOnVoCDTGfzDpIlDESmj9_gNIAlFTW1Jm6Ez_-4ik8zE6NBXns-V-dRVd8AxejKuYiBrxied_bm7JQ3jHbg1oEVYRNxBIAy17nI1bc8WaqXMvFynl1nPQFXTN9VbpIw==>  for the creation of the Orange Ad Market <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0nqUy0EG2_QD52BHgIbBOYCadsAE-XyyWnXSOpYHKgY1IdbwTkAja420H26szrGssR5F-XPp1dwBLh46mkuaJeWGbr3C1WUJfWpBdoE3BBGk1lIqqwDcA1t> . From the release: "Orange has deep relationships with both buyers and sellers of online media, and programmatic buying is becoming a key part of our digital media strategy to serve their needs," said Stephanie Hospital, EVP of Orange's Audience and Advertising division. Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0mwvF7S8EavEexpC5sIlYcQrEkk3WaS55BLCv44FAdruLmZ2c5Byh7EeWROyrgsdwMBmXzG49MgoFo0nwAHObawY0VDLsk8TUM6GPmCDEyhjNyiw6nK_fyE3wCjtU0CB4QfiIBhfWuTqYiuOYHnwpm7BEMD8pSplCTpS1BjjvyXUEyUyeci7ydGNn90Rn1MfPJguwFgzN8F2ns_gUy3SdWY6ATn-L0dvbepABX6Duz_OQ==>  


USA Today Ad Revamp


USA Today was considered revolutionary when it came to newsprint design 30 years ago. The Gannett flagship's website hasn't exactly been known for rewriting the rules, at least according to its look. But the latest redesign, while aimed for mainstream consumers, is also intended to appeal to major brands. Among other things, the redesign will de-emphasize the traditional 300x250 display formats a bit in favor of larger, more engaging ads. "I think the full-page digital ad will be the primary one of the future," Larry Kramer, USAT's president and publisher, told AdAge's Jason Del Rey. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0mfCxLN-ZmchZ84a8ot8YKZmKoFGUeTCNUx6I91P5I9PTFarYPPfBxdaCrqNEHJUw7Hgim7PDm_GmOd4HSlZ9ah4j4EbOW8tIjLI9Ai1D8OoJ7wwxi6NJh7S5zPVTWwyr9O8mfEDlzpINMc8g8pC0B4Re0feZEFTEiXjYsfsVoM_2t9iIq1sKXuLMNMDgyTcUkYPR2FjIUU7g==> . 


10,000 Flavors of TV

TV channels have multiplied to such a degree that our channels now have channels, and that's a problem, says Dave Morgan writing for Medipost. "Audience fragmentation makes buying media harder and more complex. You need to evaluate more media choices. You need to maintain more relationships. You need to traffic more ad spots to more partners. You have more competition for larger properties. Per-campaign reach goes down." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0l71mc-njSVffKPKaRswbpgNn5aP0M1N72mZTZVjtJVjnxMl31G2CDQXZcD578yhf1QH9BuTc97AZeWjN9evFTt5KTErRCxSo0Gqshz-HduyqBI8FdQGBYaJZ9Alwku_2GS2FuHxnySnDxski9P_LbL6CCFa35mkXFV7zNiDYVl4-eCicVq_C082aAkSntMVXiRCEtvvsxvVjwDQqwo7SNOx5ua1NmkbYQ=>  


Email Lockout


"A funny thing happened on the way to the Private Exchange," Dave Hendricks writes in a column on ClickZ. Well, it's not so funny if you're a fan of email ad targeting. "While thousands of pages of yesterday's news ended up in the private exchanges - articles written weeks or months ago with supposedly long tails - the freshest and hottest content put together by the same editors couldn't get in the private exchange club." Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0kF29FueIq1NhzCjsNn45nN3JaQpHh5wFeZh12UpAH79hJp31f8YMkIkMfugzkHEU8gPygnNf8Tna2oPx5HcPITjtrNpQD2IoEa53fUElTRZvYgr2TnECsB5N_OvgV67g53oUeJ2ryuaJzSqmIGVKlheSuPeNTZRGQ0bqRMMxU8kLVINg5Q7wljESNUH5Vot9ILmhKjaOiWXQ==> . 


Ecommerce Fever


For investors, Citi analyst Mark Mahaney reviews Shop.org's recent summit with the heading that "Large Retailers & Tech Ecosystems Continue [Their] Tug O' War." Ecommerce continues to "hockey stick" if you go by this: "Attendance for this annual event has increased 10x since 2002 to more than 4,500 attendees from a large number of Internet, Technology, and Retail industry participants including eBay, Google, Facebook, Toys R Us, Nordstrom, Target, Oracle, Macys, Kohl's, BazaarVoice, and DemandWare." Mahaney also referenced a Kara Swisher-moderated panel at the event where Swisher wondered aloud why Amazon was not present. 


Agencies Scoring Vendors


Digiday follows up its ad tech chaos and publishers piece <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0lZgf7vl5kmXYhS7pqGu6hOsPYYTdvC-UK8Yk_UYZ0AcQEoODKwVgp-yB1JNI8Swvspo8fFg3jJcqvWwEQDd6wlL9DIsIxbuokDvwWSqkVk8XGCH0JQEyYIeSu4xLmsVdJERN9MH1YKfPKprfEGp4vPbjMVq_SrcifKxGOnM4LuVJX1LO3FJj-Y>  with a focus on how ad agencies are dealing with vendors. Digiday's Brian Morrissey talks to VivaKi exec Mac Delaney among others for answers: "VivaKi's mission includes striking Publicis-wide deals with many vendors. As part of those agreements, Delaney's team puts the vendors through a 243-point evaluation. The criteria varies, but for a data provider, for instance, it would zero in on just where exactly its data id coming from." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0lZsmpqrqMyJ0nS9wtenHr_AXF8WgF4slKhTNUq9oWBEExfyPsZr0Vfy3tdkyne9pz9WAYus8O-RhSOu5UlmUYzwk3gKuB_CEcrFd0M_jQ4VXpJd9NbscbZolfxTJ4XoXCagQ7zX79E-avxgz2QYXfvBfbYVD-uM2s=> . 


CRM Retargeting


Matching email address to display ad cookies is becoming a hot(ter) topic. In an opinion piece on Ad Age, LiveRamp's Travis May reviews CRM Retargeting - an offering near and dear to the Rapleaf-owned company (AdExchanger 2011 Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001t1NPgeHec0nPJRY2Ole4VJsDGpilKZ2yGWLm36W4vNaBFjeUNXpV3h_IauHAfaDPYaFU4on5E_eHwaEemG_ZlbpnJwow2fgmlp797sjdsAUHaZ6IQCdn-IhW2tfZRY_u22ERAabqy8QdcJjZLL7H81AWxV16uj2XqFvzX02ukMQ=> &A). May offers a use case, "Consider a large marketer like a wireless carrier. Their CRM contains a customer's email address, what devices the customer has purchased, the lifetime value of the customer, and other key information about the customer. When their subscription is ending and it's time for the customer to likely buy a new device, the carrier would traditionally send a direct mail campaign and email marketing campaign customized for that individual. With CRM retargeting..." Yahoo! Cash


AllThingsD's Kara Swisher says that Yahoo! is about to enjoy a huge, $7 billion windfall thanks to the sale of 80% of its Alibaba stake. Swisher suggests acquisitions are ahead for Yahoo! Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_v0JA7iCQ_a6Q6A4OCZpgFIzgfjRmtfakbsOX4owO_oglspqJeWbfb7RPcrRDyw2ikNSimaa62WmaEG7te2F2yQcZn6KdSUvi8PwvZCpiU2cl71MGHor6EBY-FUZpQaG63eqCCgGp39QR2mpTnBNeuwt2GuRLcsTPi36CicoQvCRCNRKw7Otb5zjr4pa7FM6PKGzLD0ceqTmsBbyg_lwpzQ5Ms9-5x3yVkxYUicSCHdudOh0BdXEcpOtIkHvbHc6So=>  Will advertising and marketing technology lure Yahoo! CEO Marissa Mayer to use her new war chest? Hard to say how that might look. Now that Right Media has been "reaffirmed <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_tyLoD6Og_vzhPvgU-iVq3YaClylClbQRbCrCRBcic9Qat6ICyzVDuHiFN49dkpsEtRITAOxpuaGS76hLHX7ZuiIz8e5HVcpR7Rfq5tp1k-5SLqNzD0hWfGzHgo2ztUYjgvu2LotsULDfUmdYt5TVWZ7_V_WG63r6w-0OGvcWW7b17Bhi6bsXjskDV915WGoB-3IQJ5fpOATd7aKD3_qXz6> ," it is either time to invest in RMX via acquisition or more manpower to prepare for the continued growth of programmatic buying - guaranteed, remnant, Tier 1, Tier 2, etc. 


AdWords Apps Play


Google is promising "better bids, better ads" with its latest AdWords for apps offering - just in time for Apple's big iPhone announcement. The new features let marketers include reviews and ratings, similar to Amazon rankings. "We've found that when app advertisers provide users with this kind of important information about their apps, many have seen their cost per conversion decrease by about 25 percent," says Chrix Finne, Product Manager for Google Mobile Ads, in a blog post. Read it <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_sL3frwGPlWetcBwGuYsJ2Ll4a2XmY8QmrCQfxj5tOSkQ1eWv3Xx1rUJBKSljPZ0oyfYYWcYKorCiPZOmoWd666IP_T-O6vR_IX8UmvHGK49t7f72H0YRsdNVcWeLPBzvVaEpFJ1ZYT-_TZiae2kFYiO91pNtniX8N4LUZNLPtCtp9eVA6-oqUB> . 


All Social Nets Are Not Equal


When we talk about social networking and marketing, we're mostly talking about Facebook and Twitter, with LinkedIn, Pinterest and Tumblr on deck as possible platforms to augment ad messages. The trick isn't to wait until obvious business models materialize, however. Using social media is a matter of the right tool for the right job, Diane Kegley, CMO of RichRelevance tells Mediapost's Gavin O'Malley. "Not all channels in the social space are created equal," Kegley, noting that Facebook dominates as a traffic driver, pushing users to 86 percent of shopping sessions, while Pinterest and Twitter trail far behind with an 11.3 percent and 2.9 percent share, respectively. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_tOfDxT2xxBa09O5Mtgx_3Azl5t1kCmW198r8BjH382RCkKqwVSRhWSy8wNLsGrv896voYDHD78l6k-tV1d6uj_Icj8Di9aStjOi4ZnhTBphg0ny9Iba9gWQSmLRaOUoCmFmVXd9ocEZyREArCPFn7AfDGWV7zOG6g_NJEltMlToJzylZBtfaEwcr62vob_wcDpCoZ8xO2vrrGzF_l2aziWnlrA25KETMxi_cdQwvBxa-2i58TlM_alogJDvwDtNCrrWWJx2MCTEA==> .

Tag management company Ensighten (AdExchanger Q <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_uqgaqspM3SEKae-Sdj_a7obra1dwjUOCjVnWfr8VBNwKRdj3ULcCJR44ZqKvwab7hhvZKp_dT6SouVvMIPG55nY46rULVOvhbYC-GByfwzhzu0PEmF6DXzXBjiw0V21xcoY6o1SEBK7zav8jtuulpGmlecm6bjQ6peypIyjqkeb55uVn14g7w0j9uXa1yuO0IxscHzWZeaUXuR3ePUF-Nw> &A from May) raised a healthy $15.5 Million in series A funding according to a release. The company touts its traction with eCommerce publishers and says that clients include A&E Networks, LendingTree, Lenovo, Microsoft Stores, Monster and a bunch of others. Chaos


On Digiday, Josh Sternberg talks to Gawker's Erin Pettigrew and Reuters' Vikram Somaya about their overall views on ad tech vendors as they sift through solutions for each of their companies. Pettigrew says, "I want to know if we are a pawn in their takeover-the-world strategy or a partner in their service platform. I want to know if they are funded and founded by folks who are looking to flip in which case the future of our relationship would be less clear and potentially undesirable." Read more. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_ssLoNeK0e9BrtjiiuOfJPARyrCW_hjpLVY64xP_88dYviEwpVlVqNhVi506lBXTGuSCKcsx_g-A-Pwi61tNZ6NioxPsd2otW3YdARKP9_awqBilVz_xi1BkzaubbP9-QpfdLdGu8VJ0q_43bwVH2giE-lV7DFCoMcVqPglZFs-fovEm8YUF3E2>  


Platform Arms Race


It may seem that ad tech companies have too many products, that result in a lot of confusion. Who's platform is better? James Curran, co-founder of AdStaq, tells Clickz's Tim Nichols that there's an arms race among platform tools, and ultimately, the benefits will be shown. "There is value in every one of these technologies... It is the reason why ad networks flourished with high margins, great targeting and scale. None of that would be possible without technology behind it." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_vRO-rKdEV6cM86a0EYpSyY6iPsgp_tzEIFqmnTD2BhXHOcx_U2GzYdc9ue5lXXe_GUgM4lRG51OBRgm3Z7yi2_ObJa4RBCOKcxXfeAJb3ViplUMi8YP-fa5o8DutEC6626sUXfo8O8c-lB2K439HRZlqADKQLu6Pqxd-ItXx3DScGOfNSm5E-MYrnb8oDxp0Et3vQzffnOMX9VoWl1Y1y71g-vxCzZ2ttzCgAxrr1TpS5VGrXPaU2YBQyWXqN93C2xBVyC4chu0dQbrIUc2eSgpEJQzJ3a5xJLO7RrRuFHnpkUcTuWbJOswZV-W8F73fvE2evX4Kc_Di3_PeTqv5BoJpNJIG17JGnSOleJNYr2ylOMflqI8N4F> . 


Displaying The Numbers


In case you haven't seen it, comScore decided it didn't like the way it's display ad, reach rankings were breaking out and is trying something new - ad networks and web properties are now separated. The release last month (PDF) <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_tx1lVjbfTTyRa5x4waakkkaveMyJ8OW_qBaXnr9InRiJyNf_jibQyANMJFNFTuKAgPSFc_Ha27_TKmOI3uTF_uKYNk3X1AH5KTSpHeGm81tB7PB2ywHckXHGJJu9VDDBaxBJg4SfT4zSycaeKRwKLoc55bW-X1PRmAkNgc7MPw4gzdDbbMM2LntNl_HN5EgmrIrDiqTv_LCrux4nJKcnJQe68L0A1AOLkSzO83smDTR-uc26FwQYYXGwVlArIxr_v_FB6gWJ5sTVl4RMIv4VAfEJDN1hvkgloMu6NzVCpSW-AWQrnOjWFJEwXqkRfhT2Y=>  explained the the company has "expanded its display ad ecosystem reporting to provide additional granularity in the classification of ad publishers, networks and other platforms that comprise the ecosystem." Get this month's pay-for-play numbers <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_uTgfUouQI7cpw36DurxXU6auY9tuoHXp_SMDJip7dMjr8r2RyvDsYyuP3WyDqOjQcpZj9ufjZOoJL35WB5A_dUv2AFrfoFhLoxvJkMwBoCNwIY__OjzC9HvztKC8z44_5qSI5_4dLlLLUbKkBDDFGN630QMP_7VZDIDIQasytmmtVRUFDlehQYZgHX7XLmqGrqCpz-1VCsuFNRAXaXjFOwZ4TczrGdkRotqTWZlGumiFrqvQ0KEGgOzw94P2bS-is=>  which say that PulsePoint is at the top of all the U.S. ad networks on a reach basis. 


Growth Hacking


Buzz phrase! LeadsCon empresario Jay Weintraub wades into the "growth hacking" discussion, a concept popularized by Andrew Chen <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_tM6fAWz4I9ILB1H72GFM7SasGdgO3oakh8r5b9Y0htJRUtmzy6Tm-E9Uc6UevmqWs4hYQSzqQbusCOPRpkgvub5mRzjAFJS8GSKFyvNfCE6Sx1v7iJUDJY0YVnnlvGhqBG6App8E4KPqK8MX8-bMllY8QKRbtEr1DuLcGHmTw2LEl5HuEyerrPP3Bev3nj-R_4vh1bZDIUEA==> . He writes, "Today's customer acquisition techniques and platforms were once new, and unlocking them most effectively, ultimately meant doing so programmatically. That is why I tend to think of customer acquisition as the systematic scaling of strategies uncovered during the growth hacking process. If you can figure out the latter, it gives you a leg up on the former." Read what that means. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001NTA4QQT6Q_vhk9XjPyRK9XnuGiA9ekXMLvlxDtaTpSi9m-BM8Qz_dOrMDHvg39J7AxTrnln8ARyyiZ1VTqrfRjhYc3hWzQkPLoRck3Tue6QJ1rAUTRnevhhGNwHhht0T55pEt-k757ObCbo7Oezhza9ueZbQgPAfzN0OA5n_7kGq-qDf1z6G7puY_uwftwrs>

Social Matchmaker


Facebook is letting some large advertisers match its users to their CRM databases using an email address or phone number. AdAge contrasts it to similar standard practices in the magazine industry, posing the question, do people want or expect this from Facebook? '"I don't think anyone who has given an email and phone number to Facebook expected it to be used by Tide to target ads at them," privacy policy consultant Alan Chapell tells Michael Learmonth. Read more.  <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK4dtEa4_HcuSG_yswF_uYIuwU0M74pCLWyFgH98oMVv669SduzGufsngCAGJg3uPF28EQw5WwuFq2BedCPxS17mHj_Afmq7Fd5wJmEDcdMBo9eUkBHwv5x-ZEw63O65TLQwau0Hgr1GW92uYWkLA3RSh4ft_wjL0DOnFAIBkVoAJ-rQ2LRdCeviB7a9jO10yJL7Zwg8qIxWtgbsBiNlWzPZ2l7i3tP_sTdaKf3R1p7M2mdKAI3xCb-VF0MExrK-0ASMPvQUVXUyjmlX58-ihs7ic2AEZqiKeas0491gqBNLl3GHMK3Ym8FSoNj4WjnxEPsg_6X0qAQR_r01oPqt6XpjyQ-xrv4gxmS8FVwjKeJfU5ENNek-1Msgw-cOt1Hv61TFGvM0AOdxEA==> 


Don't Ask, Don't Track


The uproar <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK4Qa0cug8P5pnRGLxapOSliMC1q_mleiqODGoVxvEO0sHS8PlXZPj1pkJDvOy3QoyKyFnoJlbmMh3xYaZqJOCS_AZvNjYf5O8G3cqLKbSu6GNFbSDYRgsU9Nx7swLolLKzHGw1B6TZyXFq5G5pem3ThiCRXnPAwOyHaeIJXX7SwjhP14eOOotWH>  in the online ad industry over Microsoft's decision to make "do not track" the default position of its latest version of the Internet Explorer browser left some observers wondering how the advertising side of the Redmond software giant viewed that move. Rik van der Kooi, corporate VP of Microsoft's Advertising Business Group, writes in Adweek that the decision reflects a new way of thinking about how to pursue consumers in an age of increasing privacy worries: "We need a new norm. No longer should the consumers who generate the data for our industry be left out of the equation. On the contrary, they should have the option to participate in that part of the business to a greater extent than they ever have before." Read the rest <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK61lPdo47eYt2pb11KD0vmTxJ6rt55ISvLcyFhlQpFE9Kq68FmrhAJYGMALafgt3pgMuFcnrlliy7AsdM1Db2AQmVYz6xWBGXHjoZmRIOUOh8h8CFWiwj5-qdfdkVEIlqDbHh5V7nn3RCw7ofkoEdVCuyo5MBXM4dadZZLiJXCHlSw8C-OapwZ7> . 


Track 'N Shop


Fast Company's Neal Ungerleider profile's Swarm, which can track brick & mortar shoppers via their smartphones' use of in-store wi-fi. By tracking shoppers looking at prices, stores can customers coupons in real-time as they track their movements. "Every customer we talk to, from small retailers to national chains, has the same problem. None of them actually know what's happening in their stores in real time; we can help with that," says Swarm EVP Ryan Denehy. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK6Dnzm-jkp4NidJQ0HxshcnlUMEaigBUM-21q5HSB0h0cz1NU61h2hMoxrTC0j73_zFq97GRg6xLTpLr-sX0Y1HU1yHR2C9p4jV76PIHiITGcsVDoDzsgna_fVOslt08c_QaEBXIUrLEpkfPK6411nkLKbpvYVVOfYXBaT4-7aDb7JzMIUv3XJfzCbkp9ssvdjLJUDIJaH2mw==> . 


Once Again, From the Top


To bastardize a well-known saying, the market for someone to simplify the display ad tech landscape is infinite. Simpli.fi CRO James Moore takes a shot at this beloved genre with his own breakdown of the space, grouping companies under well known classifications (DSPs, SSPs/exchanges) and some less familiar ones (performance enhancement companies, anyone?) He acknowledges, "Change is inevitable and the neat buckets I have constructed for you are beginning to leak." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK4WflNFc-f-DNGoP6rP2Lg9S22dq5m2wdTl9K6j2ZuA3gPx510EOyuZDKlcTLohwe9dqQ3o23355UO4D53ktOfAYaTIuCK0_lxycpIrhO8R0XVASZp8WKnKzXrl7PdxO3atZ4maZjXsXV6c7SdQfKZuQqA8Pg8dW4mP9Gbu8T6ni5lnf5Lu3gGo9_RQ29n2b4Vbgq6hffvglaUdxe6z6OYD>  


RTB for Mobile


On his personal blog, Google-Admeld-er and mobile guru Marc Theerman takes time out to make a quick post on Facebook's new exchange. He writes <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK77dP4HyUeVAj27fVsjUTUwQU2SBR8Zr5_zSM1lDPGI1T4BgHIlB4zhIu4hTtYGaPeJaVTvMlZJMnbi-kqk9GvVNNiezq_908QuOod2dNjAIMep4VTpey5TGN5xWXgA8vE=> , "FBX is a a real-time bidding ad system where visitors to third-party websites are marked with a cookie, and can then be shown real-time bid ads related to their web browsing when they return to Facebook. Thats mildly interesting for desktop, but potentially game changing for mobile. More to come I am sure." 


Getting Acquired


Chris Dixon review his notes on the acquisition process for startups on his personal blog. He begins, "There is an old saying that startups are bought not sold. Clearly it is better to be in high demand and have inbound interest. But for product and tech acquisitions especially, it is often about getting the attention of the right people at the acquirer. Sometimes the right person is corp dev, other times product or business unit leads, and other times C-level management." Read it. <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?e=001obdaifChUK4uf9WIsKOVi2e7q_AT4mNFuBYH1FSY66srIrRuy0Sso0StbSk0Fguz9lBZNrXkVEW_XYKxpjbpho0fSqkCbDktTx86b9TkvbZiZ1dh-wEdyohk_LMrxvhWAVvAJxmJNcNFQbiE_kTW-FfyAZX3SYnVbZJeSYT9d6LvHXFv9CJFSw==>
